<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h1><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ory documentation is the single source of truth for usage, implementation,
configuration, and troubleshooting of the Ory Network and all projects of the
<a href="https://www.ory.com/docs/ecosystem/projects/" rel="nofollow">Ory Ecosystem</a>. The documentation
is best consumed through the
<a href="https://www.ory.com/docs/" rel="nofollow">Ory documentation portal</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">To see the source code of each of the projects, visit the project repository:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/kratos/">Ory Kratos</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/hydra/">Ory Hydra</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/oathkeeper/">Ory Oathkeeper</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/keto/">Ory Keto</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Documentation of other Ory projects:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/k8s/tree/master/docs/helm">Ory Kubernetes Helm Charts</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/dockertest/blob/v3/README.md">Ory Dockertest</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ory/sdk/blob/master/README.md">Ory SDKs</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Style guide</h1><a id="user-content-style-guide" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Style guide" href="#style-guide"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This style guide outlines the most important rules and conventions that apply to
the Ory documentation. If there are no Ory-specific requirements or guidelines
for a given topic, refer to the
<a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/style-guide/welcome/" rel="nofollow">Microsoft Writing Style Guide</a>
and follow the rules described there.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Grammar and style</h2><a id="user-content-grammar-and-style" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Grammar and style" href="#grammar-and-style"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ory documentation must be clear, concise, and unambiguous. To achieve that,
follow these simple rules:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Use active voice and present tense.</li>
<li>Always write in American English.</li>
<li>Use
<a href="https://www.ef.com/wwen/english-resources/english-grammar/zero-conditional/" rel="nofollow">zero conditional</a>
when talking about the cause-and-effect in software behavior.</li>
<li>Use the right words to make sure that your message is clear and unambiguous.
Don't use words like "should", "could", or "may".</li>
<li>Don't use phrasal verbs, colloquialisms, and jargon.</li>
<li>Don't refer to users in ways that imply their sex.</li>
<li>Don't use contractions of Latin origins such as <code>e.g</code> or <code>i.e</code>.</li>
<li>Remember to use articles (<code>a</code>, <code>an</code>, <code>the</code>) in your writing.</li>
<li>Use common contractions such as <code>aren't</code>, <code>don't</code>, <code>doesn't</code> to sound
friendly and informal.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Lists</h3><a id="user-content-lists" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Lists" href="#lists"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ory follows the
<a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/style-guide/scannable-content/lists" rel="nofollow">Microsoft Writing Style Guide list formatting guidelines</a>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>List items must begin with a capital letter unless there's a specific reason
not to do that. For example, the item is a proper name that's not capitalized,
a parameter, or a command wrapped in backticks (<code>`</code>).</li>
<li>Don't use punctuation such as commas (<code>,</code>), semicolons (<code>;</code>), or conjunctions
(<code>and</code>, <code>or</code>) at the end of list items.</li>
<li>Use periods (<code>.</code>) only at the end of list items that are proper sentences,
even very short ones.</li>
<li>Make list items consistent in structure. For example, if one list item is a
full sentence, make all list items full sentences. Don't use different
structures for list items in a single list.</li>
<li>Indent lines with 3 spaces to denote nested sub-items in lists. Indent text,
code blocks, and images.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Headings</h3><a id="user-content-headings" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Headings" href="#headings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use
<a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/style-guide/text-formatting/using-type/use-sentence-style-capitalization" rel="nofollow">sentence case</a>
for headings.</li>
<li>The highest heading level in documents is <code>h2</code>. Use <code>h1</code> only when you
override the document <code>title</code>.</li>
<li>The lowest heading level in documents is <code>h4</code>. If you absolutely need to add
more heading levels, don't go lower than <code>h5</code>.</li>
<li>Avoid using symbols and special characters in headings.</li>
<li>Leave one blank line before and after a heading.</li>
<li>Don't use links in headings.</li>
<li>Headings play an important role in SEO and searchability and make the document
more scannable. Make your headings short and true to the content they
introduce.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Formatting</h2><a id="user-content-formatting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Formatting" href="#formatting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Write in <a href="https://www.markdownguide.org/" rel="nofollow">Markdown</a>. Don't mix HTML tags with
Markdown. Files with the <code>.mdx</code> extension use
<a href="https://mdxjs.com/" rel="nofollow">JSX-extended Markdown (MDX)</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Document front matter</h3><a id="user-content-document-front-matter" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Document front matter" href="#document-front-matter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Add this front matter to every document you create:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
id: excellent_feature
title: Learn how to use the excellent feature in your implementation
sidebar_label: Excellent feature
slug: excellent-feature-for-some-reason
---"><pre><span class="pl-s">---</span>
<span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">excellent_feature</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Learn how to use the excellent feature in your implementation</span>
<span class="pl-ent">sidebar_label</span>: <span class="pl-s">Excellent feature</span>
<span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">excellent-feature-for-some-reason</span>
<span class="pl-s">---</span></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>id</code> is the document identifier that makes up the last part of the document
URL. Try to come up with a short ID that accurately describes the content. IDs
that use multiple words must use hyphens (<code>-</code>) to separate the words.</li>
<li><code>title</code> is the document title that’s displayed as the page header. Used by
search engines when displaying search results. Try to make it descriptive so
that it helps readers understand what the document is about at the first
glance. If it comes out long(ish), you can overwrite it by adding a <code>h1</code> in
the very first line following the front matter. Use sentence case.</li>
<li><code>sidebar_label</code> represents the document title used in the sidebar (left
navigation). Create a short document title that fits the sidebar width. Use
sentence case.</li>
<li><code>slug</code> is an optional property that allows you to customize the document URL.
Use it to create more meaningful, SEO-friendly URLs.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bolding, 'code formatting'</h3><a id="user-content-bolding-code-formatting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bolding, 'code formatting'" href="#bolding-code-formatting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use only <code>code</code> and <strong>bold</strong> formatting. Don't use any other formatting.</li>
<li>For inline code, wrap text in single backticks (<code>`</code>). For code blocks use
three backticks (<code>```</code>)</li>
<li>Use <code>code</code> formatting for:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Commands, for example <code>ory --help</code></li>
<li>File names and paths, for example <code>file.txt</code>, <code>~/Desktop/git/docs</code></li>
<li>Environment variables, for example <code>CUSTOM_ENV_VAR</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Use <strong>bold</strong> only when writing about user interface (UI) elements.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Linking</h3><a id="user-content-linking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linking" href="#linking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Link to external web pages using absolute links. Don't expose the link on its
own. Instead, embed it in descriptive text. For example:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Ory documentation uses [Prism syntax highlighting](https://prismjs.com/)."><pre class="notranslate"><code>Ory documentation uses [Prism syntax highlighting](https://prismjs.com/).
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Link to documents within this repository using relative links. When
referencing the file, use the file name.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[Some link](../path/to/file.mdx)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[Some link](../path/to/file.mdx)
</code></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Code blocks</h3><a id="user-content-code-blocks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Code blocks" href="#code-blocks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Always add a programming language identifier to code blocks. Ory documentation
uses <a href="https://prismjs.com/" rel="nofollow">Prism syntax highlighting</a>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```json
{some-JSON-code-here}
```"><pre class="notranslate"><code>```json
{some-JSON-code-here}
```
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">For command line examples, use <code>shell</code> as the programming language identifier.
Don't put <code>$</code> before the command.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```shell
ory get identities
```"><pre class="notranslate"><code>```shell
ory get identities
```
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">For Ory Permissions (Keto) relation tuples, use <code>keto-relation-tuples</code>
language identifier, and for relationships use <code>keto-relationships</code>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```keto-relation-tuples
namespace:object#relation:subject
// comment
```

```keto-relationships
namespace:subject is relation of object
is namespace:subject allowed to permission on object?
// comment
```"><pre class="notranslate"><code>```keto-relation-tuples
namespace:object#relation:subject
// comment
```

```keto-relationships
namespace:subject is relation of object
is namespace:subject allowed to permission on object?
// comment
```
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">For multi-line commands, indent subsequent lines of the command with two
spaces.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```shell
curl --request GET -sL \
  --header &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \
  --header &quot;Authorization: Bearer {ORY_API_KEY}&quot; \
  'https://{project-slug}.projects.oryapis.com/admin/identities/{identity_id}?include_credential=oidc'
```"><pre class="notranslate"><code>```shell
curl --request GET -sL \
  --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
  --header "Authorization: Bearer {ORY_API_KEY}" \
  'https://{project-slug}.projects.oryapis.com/admin/identities/{identity_id}?include_credential=oidc'
```
</code></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Placeholders and dummy data</h3><a id="user-content-placeholders-and-dummy-data" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Placeholders and dummy data" href="#placeholders-and-dummy-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Using placeholders and dummy data in code snippets and command examples is a
good way to ensure that users run commands in the context of their setups and,
as a result, achieve success faster. Additionally, this fabricated information
prevents leaking of sensitive data such as tokens or API keys.</p>
<p dir="auto">Follow these rules when using placeholders and dummy data:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Introduce placeholders and dummy data in curly brackets with a preceding $ so
they can be used in bash commands.</li>
<li>Use colons (<code>-</code>) or underscores (<code>_</code>) to separate multiple words, for example
<code>{ORY_SESSION_COOKIE}</code> or <code>{project-slug}</code>.</li>
<li>When referring to a project API URL or SDK URL, always use
<code>https://$PROJECT_SLUG.projects.oryapis.com</code>.</li>
<li>When referring to scenarios in which the user runs a custom domain, use
<code>https://ory.your-custom-domain.com</code>.</li>
<li>Always use short, but descriptive, verbal placeholders. Don't mix digits and
letters to mimic the format of the data you mock.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">UI references</h3><a id="user-content-ui-references" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: UI references" href="#ui-references"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When talking about any user interface (UI) in the Ory documentation, follow
these rules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>When referring to UI elements, always use the exact text associated with the
given element.</li>
<li>Format the name of the UI element you refer to in <strong>bold</strong>.</li>
<li>Format any user input with <code>code</code>.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Example: In the <strong>Identity Model Schema</strong> box, type <code>MyCustomIdentitySchema</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Diagrams</h3><a id="user-content-diagrams" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Diagrams" href="#diagrams"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use <a href="https://mermaid-js.github.io/mermaid/#/" rel="nofollow">Mermaid</a> to create diagrams. You
can run the tool locally or use <a href="https://mermaid.live" rel="nofollow">Mermaid Live Editor</a> in
the browser. See the
<a href="https://jojozhuang.github.io/tutorial/mermaid-cheat-sheet/" rel="nofollow">Mermaid Cheatsheet</a>
for a detailed description on how to use Mermaid.</p>
<p dir="auto">To add a Mermaid diagram, use this <code>mdx-code-block</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```mdx-code-block
import Mermaid from &quot;@site/src/theme/Mermaid&quot;
&lt;Mermaid
  chart={`

{your-Mermaid-code}

`}
/&gt;
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">mdx-code-block</span><span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">import Mermaid from "@site/src/theme/Mermaid"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;Mermaid</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  chart={`</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">{your-Mermaid-code}</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">`}</span>
<span class="pl-c1">/&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span><span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Import &amp; reference content</h2><a id="user-content-import--reference-content" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Import &amp; reference content" href="#import--reference-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Markdown partials</h3><a id="user-content-markdown-partials" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Markdown partials" href="#markdown-partials"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If a certain piece of content must be re-used across multiple documents in the
exact form, it's a good idea to turn it into a partial. Thanks to that, you
maintain content in a single file, instead of multiple instances of the same
content in many docs.</p>
<p dir="auto">Add partials to the <code>_common</code> directory.</p>
<p dir="auto">To import a partial, use this <code>mdx-code-block</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```mdx-code-block
import ExamplePartial from './_common/example.md'

&lt;ExamplePartial /&gt;
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">mdx-code-block</span><span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">import ExamplePartial from './_common/example.md'</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;ExamplePartial /&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span><span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>TIP:</strong> Headings contained in partials aren't added to the Docusaurus table
of contents (ToC). To make sure users can access all headings through the ToC,
don't add headings to partials. Instead, add appropriate headings to the
document manually and introduce partials after them. To see an implementation
of this approach, look at
<a href="https://github.com/ory/docs/blob/0137302d511b2a6b0e17a570e917d92fcdff1d1f/docs/kratos/social-signin/10_google.mdx?plain=1#L237">this file</a>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Code snippets</h3><a id="user-content-code-snippets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Code snippets" href="#code-snippets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">From GitHub</h4><a id="user-content-from-github" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: From GitHub" href="#from-github"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use
<a href="https://github.com/ory/docusaurus-template/blob/master/src/theme/CodeFromRemote.js">CodeFromRemote</a>
to import code directly from GitHub.</p>
<p dir="auto">Use this <code>mdx-code-block</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```mdx-code-block
import CodeFromRemote from '@theme/CodeFromRemote'

&lt;CodeFromRemote
  lang=&quot;js&quot;
  link=&quot;https://github.com/ory/kratos-selfservice-ui-node/blob/master/src/middleware/simple.ts&quot;
  src=&quot;https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ory/kratos-selfservice-ui-node/master/src/middleware/simple.ts&quot;
  startAt=&quot;{CONTENT_FROM_CODE}&quot;
  endAt=&quot;{CONTENT_FROM_CODE}&quot;
/&gt;
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">mdx-code-block</span><span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">import CodeFromRemote from '@theme/CodeFromRemote'</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;CodeFromRemote</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  lang="js"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  link="https://github.com/ory/kratos-selfservice-ui-node/blob/master/src/middleware/simple.ts"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ory/kratos-selfservice-ui-node/master/src/middleware/simple.ts"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  startAt="{CONTENT_FROM_CODE}"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">  endAt="{CONTENT_FROM_CODE}"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">/&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span><span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>lang</code> specifies the programming language the code is in</li>
<li><code>link</code> is the file location displayed in the top part of the code block window</li>
<li><code>src</code> is the direct link used to import the code (optional)</li>
<li><code>startAt</code> , <code>endAt</code> are used to define where the imported snippet starts and
ends (optional)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">From this repository</h4><a id="user-content-from-this-repository" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: From this repository" href="#from-this-repository"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```mdx-code-block
import CodeBlock from '@theme/CodeBlock'
import exampleJs from '!!raw-loader!./code-example.jsx'
import exampleGo from '!!raw-loader!./code-example.go'

&lt;CodeBlock className=&quot;language-jsx&quot;&gt;{exampleJs}&lt;/CodeBlock&gt;
&lt;CodeBlock className=&quot;language-go&quot;&gt;{exampleGo}&lt;/CodeBlock&gt;
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">mdx-code-block</span><span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">import CodeBlock from '@theme/CodeBlock'</span>
<span class="pl-c1">import exampleJs from '!!raw-loader!./code-example.jsx'</span>
<span class="pl-c1">import exampleGo from '!!raw-loader!./code-example.go'</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;CodeBlock className="language-jsx"&gt;{exampleJs}&lt;/CodeBlock&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;CodeBlock className="language-go"&gt;{exampleGo}&lt;/CodeBlock&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span><span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Screenshots and videos</h2><a id="user-content-screenshots-and-videos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Screenshots and videos" href="#screenshots-and-videos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use screenshots and videos sparingly. These resources tend to get out-of-date
quickly and are cumbersome to maintain.</li>
<li>Screenshots and videos must capture only the relevant parts of the screen.</li>
<li>Screenshots and videos must capture UI elements in English. If you’re
capturing parts of the browser UI in your work, make sure the UI is in
English.</li>
<li>Make an effort to get the screenshots and videos looking as clean as possible.
Avoid situations where text fields suggest irrelevant inputs, avoid erratic
mouse cursor movements and general chaos.</li>
<li>You must add media to <code>_static</code> folders.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>In the <code>_static</code> directory, each document that uses media has its own
directory.</li>
<li>In the directory of the document, the files have numbers for names, for
example, <code>1.png</code>, <code>2.png</code>, <code>3.png</code>. The filenames should reflect the stage
at which the media is used in the document. This means that the screenshot
named <code>1.png</code> will be used in line 70, while the diagram <code>2.svg</code> will be
used in line 100.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compressing images</h3><a id="user-content-compressing-images" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compressing images" href="#compressing-images"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Compress images you add to the documentation to keep the repository lean. You
can use <a href="https://pngquant.org/" rel="nofollow"><code>pngquant</code></a>.
<a href="https://about.gitlab.com/blog/2020/01/30/simple-trick-for-smaller-screenshots/" rel="nofollow">Read this article to learn a trick to make your screenshots 80% smaller</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recording and compressing videos</h3><a id="user-content-recording-and-compressing-videos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recording and compressing videos" href="#recording-and-compressing-videos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We recommend using
<a href="https://support.apple.com/en-gb/guide/quicktime-player/qtp97b08e666/mac" rel="nofollow">Quicktime to record videos</a>.
Follow these rules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use 16:9 format with at least 1024 pixels of width. <code>ffmpeg</code> will scale it to
the right size.</li>
<li>Make sure that no history or auto-suggestions are visible.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">After recording the video, convert the <code>.mov</code> file to <code>mp4</code> and <code>webm</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-shell-session notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="file=&quot;screencast.mov&quot;

ffmpeg -i $file -an -c:v libvpx-vp9 -vf scale=1024:-1 -crf 30 -b:v 0 &quot;${file%.*}&quot;.webm
ffmpeg -i $file -vcodec h264 -vf scale=1024:-1 -an &quot;${file%.*}&quot;.mp4"><pre><span class="pl-c1">file="screencast.mov"</span>

<span class="pl-c1">ffmpeg -i $file -an -c:v libvpx-vp9 -vf scale=1024:-1 -crf 30 -b:v 0 "${file%.*}".webm</span>
<span class="pl-c1">ffmpeg -i $file -vcodec h264 -vf scale=1024:-1 -an "${file%.*}".mp4</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Use this <code>mdx-code-block</code> to add the video to your document:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```mdx-code-block
import mp4 from './_static/screencast.mp4'
import webm from './_static/screencast.webm'
import VideoEmbed from '@site/src/components/VideoEmbed'

&lt;VideoEmbed mp4={mp4} webm={webm} /&gt;
```"><pre class="notranslate"><code>```mdx-code-block
import mp4 from './_static/screencast.mp4'
import webm from './_static/screencast.webm'
import VideoEmbed from '@site/src/components/VideoEmbed'

&lt;VideoEmbed mp4={mp4} webm={webm} /&gt;
```
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Ory Console</h2><a id="user-content-ory-console" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Ory Console" href="#ory-console"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigate to Ory Console Pages</h3><a id="user-content-navigate-to-ory-console-pages" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigate to Ory Console Pages" href="#navigate-to-ory-console-pages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can use the <code>/current/</code> route to navigate users to their active Ory Network
project. For example, to access the Custom UI settings for the active Ory
Network project in the Console, you can link to:
<a href="https://console.ory.com/projects/current/ui" rel="nofollow">https://console.ory.com/projects/current/ui</a></p>
<p dir="auto">When referencing a page of the Ory Console, use the
<code>&lt;ConsoleLink route="project..." /&gt;</code> component in MDX files.</p>
<p dir="auto">The component resolves the navigation section and page title for the given
route, and renders a standard markup for both, as well as the link with the
<code>/current/</code> shortcut mentioned above:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;ConsoleLink route=&quot;project.activity.events&quot; /&gt;

// becomes:
// Activity → Logs &amp; Events in the [Ory Console](https://console.ory.sh/current/projects/activity/events)"><pre><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">ConsoleLink</span> <span class="pl-c1">route</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"project.activity.events"</span> <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// becomes:</span>
<span class="pl-c">// Activity → Logs &amp; Events in the [Ory Console](https://console.ory.sh/current/projects/activity/events)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">A list of all supported routes can be found here:
<a href="/ory/docs/blob/master/src/components/ConsoleLink/console-routes.ts">src/components/ConsoleLink/console-routes.ts</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please note that the syntax is like accessing a path in a JS object, but as a
string. If the route you want to reference is found in the <code>console-routes.ts</code>
file in the following way:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  project: {
    activity: {
      events: {
        route: &quot;/projects/[project]/activity/events&quot;,
      }
    }
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">project</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">activity</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">events</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">route</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/projects/[project]/activity/events"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Use <code>&lt;ConsoleLink route="project.activity.events" /&gt;</code> to reference it.</p>
<p dir="auto">To add a new route, you need to add an entry in
<a href="https://github.com/ory/docs/blob/master/src/components/ConsoleLink/console-routes.ts"><code>console-routes.ts</code></a>
as well as
<a href="https://github.com/ory/docs/blob/master/src/components/ConsoleLink/console-nav-data.ts"><code>console-nav-data.ts</code></a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Testing</h2><a id="user-content-testing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Testing" href="#testing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To test the documentation locally:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Clone this repository.</li>
<li>Navigate to the cloned repository and run <code>npm install</code> to install all
dependencies.</li>
<li>Run the development server and test the changes you made using a fully
operational version of the documentation portal that runs on your machine.
Run <code>npm run start</code>.</li>
<li>Create a production build to check for any technical issues, such as invalid
internal links. Run <code>npm run build</code>.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Redirects</h3><a id="user-content-redirects" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Redirects" href="#redirects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When the URL of a document changes, you must set up a redirect to preserve SEO
and prevent broken links. Without redirects, the original URL returns a 404
error, breaking existing links from external sites and causing search engines to
lose page authority.</p>
<p dir="auto">The rule is: if the URL in the browser changes, add a redirect. If it doesn't,
no redirect is required.</p>
<p dir="auto">Filenames don't always determine URLs. Ory documentation uses numbered prefixes
in filenames and sets URLs explicitly in the front matter. Renaming with no
other changes doesn't require a redirect because the final URL stays the same.</p>
<p dir="auto">You must add a redirect when you</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>change the <code>slug</code> or <code>id</code> property in the document front matter</li>
<li>delete a document</li>
<li>move a document to a different directory (if it changes the URL path)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to add a redirect</h4><a id="user-content-how-to-add-a-redirect" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to add a redirect" href="#how-to-add-a-redirect"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Add redirects to the vercel.json file in the repository root. Use this format:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;redirects&quot;: [
    {
      &quot;source&quot;: &quot;/docs/old-path&quot;,
      &quot;destination&quot;: &quot;/docs/new-path&quot;,
      &quot;permanent&quot;: false
    }
  ]
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"redirects"</span>: [
    {
      <span class="pl-ent">"source"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/docs/old-path<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
      <span class="pl-ent">"destination"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/docs/new-path<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
      <span class="pl-ent">"permanent"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>
    }
  ]
}</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Start with permanent: false (302 redirect) until you confirm the redirect
works in the preview or production environment.</li>
<li>Change to permanent: true (301 redirect) after you verify the redirect
functions correctly.</li>
<li>Test the redirect in the Vercel preview deployment before merging.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Formatting documentation</h2><a id="user-content-formatting-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Formatting documentation" href="#formatting-documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All documents and other files in this repository must be formatted with Prettier
using the <a href="https://github.com/ory/prettier-styles">Ory Prettier styles</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">To format all relevant files, run these commands from the main directory of the
repository:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="make format
git commit -a -m &quot;chore: format&quot;
git push"><pre>make format
git commit -a -m <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>chore: format<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
git push</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For a better workflow, install the Prettier plugin for your editor:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=esbenp.prettier-vscode" rel="nofollow">VSCode Prettier plugin</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.jetbrains.com/help/idea/prettier.html" rel="nofollow">IntelliJ Prettier plugin</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding content to "Examples" page</h2><a id="user-content-adding-content-to-examples-page" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding content to &quot;Examples&quot; page" href="#adding-content-to-examples-page"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.ory.sh/docs/getting-started/overview" rel="nofollow">The Quickstart overview</a>
provides an overview of Ory quickstarts. To add a new example or modify existing
entries:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Open <code>examples-content.tsx</code> in <code>src/pages/_assets/</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Copy the following snippet and append it to the correct array (either
official, community, or self-hosting examples):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-tsx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
      title: &quot;Protect a Page with Login: NextJs/React&quot;, //Your example title goes here
      language: &quot;typescript&quot;,                           //The main programming language of your example
      author: &quot;ory&quot;,                                    //The author's GitHub handle
      tested: true,                                     //Is the example in ory/examples or ory/docs and has automated tests?
      repo: &quot;https://github.com/ory/docs/tree/master/code-examples/protect-page-login/nextjs&quot;, //The repo containing the example code
      docs: &quot;https://www.ory.sh/docs/guides/protect-page-login/next.js&quot;,                       //Documentation for the example, can be README, blog article or similar
    },"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Protect a Page with Login: NextJs/React"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">//Your example title goes here</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">language</span>: <span class="pl-s">"typescript"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>                           <span class="pl-c">//The main programming language of your example</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">author</span>: <span class="pl-s">"ory"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>                                    <span class="pl-c">//The author's GitHub handle</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">tested</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>                                     <span class="pl-c">//Is the example in ory/examples or ory/docs and has automated tests?</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">repo</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://github.com/ory/docs/tree/master/code-examples/protect-page-login/nextjs"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">//The repo containing the example code</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">docs</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://www.ory.sh/docs/guides/protect-page-login/next.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>                       <span class="pl-c">//Documentation for the example, can be README, blog article or similar</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>language</code> can be one of: dart, django, docker, erlang, flutter, go, java,
javascript, kotlin, kubernetes, nextjs, nodejs, ory, php, python, react,
rescript, svelte, typescript, vue</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Open a pull request with your changes.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CLI and API reference - auto-generated content</h2><a id="user-content-cli-and-api-reference---auto-generated-content" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CLI and API reference - auto-generated content" href="#cli-and-api-reference---auto-generated-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ory documentation contains auto-generated content such as CLI and API
references. Documents of this type are generated from source code and are pushed
to this repository by an automated job.</p>
<p dir="auto">As such, editing any of these documents in the Ory documentation repository
isn't the way to change or fix this content. Any changes you make will be
overwritten by the next push that follows the generation process.</p>
<p dir="auto">Instead, find the lines in question in the source code of the Ory projects and
edit them there. For example, if you want to edit the documentation of the Ory
Kratos CLI, you must edit this file:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ory/kratos/blob/master/cmd/clidoc/main.go">https://github.com/ory/kratos/blob/master/cmd/clidoc/main.go</a></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>cmd/clidoc/main.go</code> is the general path for all Ory projects.</p>
<p dir="auto">The command to generate the CLI docs can be found here:
<a href="https://github.com/ory/x/blob/master/clidoc/generate.go#L96">https://github.com/ory/x/blob/master/clidoc/generate.go#L96</a></p>
</article></div><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><button hidden="" data-testid="" data-hotkey-scope="read-only-cursor-text-area"></button><button hidden=""></button></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>
